    1. Source data for this look-up tool was LAST UPDATED 07APR2021
    2. This tool searches the CONTRACT DRUG LIST (CDL) and returns items of similar therapeutic (chemical) class.
    3. If your search returns no results, the drug requested may not be part of the CDL.
    4. Certain drugs with Code 1 restrictions may not show up in this tool. It is always recommended to refer back to the CDL.
    5. If your search yields too many items, click on the HIGHLIGHT button.
    6. This will highlight the requested search term within the results.
    7. To clear the search field, click on the GARBAGE CAN button.
